#SHX annexing by CHI
country_event = {
	id = kmt.1
	title = kmt.1.t
	desc = kmt.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 608 size > 10}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 614 size > 10}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					divisions_in_state = { state = 607 size > 10}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = PRC
				factor = -100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.1.a
		CHI = {
			annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
			country_event = { id = kmt.2 }
			set_country_flag = shx_sumitted
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		name = kmt.1.b
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.3 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		name = kmt.1.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = SHX
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					is_puppet_of = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.4 days = 1 }}
		CHI = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SHX modifier = KMT_SHX_refused }}
		PRC = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SHX modifier = PRC_SHX_refused }}
		SHX = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = CHI modifier = SHX_SHX_refused }}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = refused_shx_offer
		}
	}
}

#declare internal war propaganda lost
country_event = {
	id = kmt.6
	title = kmt.6.t
	desc = kmt.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_idea = KMT_propaganda
		OR = {
			has_offensive_war_with = PRC
			has_offensive_war_with = SHX
			has_offensive_war_with = GXC
			has_offensive_war_with = XSM
			has_offensive_war_with = YUN
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	immediate = {
		CHI = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
				days = 600
			}
		}
	}
}

#Japan invades remove busted
country_event = {
	id = kmt.7
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = PRC
		}
		has_idea = KMT_propaganda_busted
		AND = {
			has_defensive_war_with = JAP
			has_offensive_war_with = CHI

		}
	}

	immediate = {
		CHI = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_propaganda_busted
		}
	}
}

#TIB offer
country_event = {
	id = kmt.8
	title = kmt.8.t
	desc = kmt.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_TIB_british_mission

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = TIB
						ratio > 0.5
					}
				}
				add = 60
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					has_war = yes
					surrender_progress > 0.1
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = kmt.8.a
		CHI = { annex_country = { target = TIB transfer_troops = no } }
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.9 }}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		name = kmt.8.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = TIB
				}
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = kmt.10 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#taiwan refused
country_event = {
	id = kmt.17
	title = kmt.17.t
	desc = kmt.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.17.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = FROM
			generator = { 524 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					ROOT = {
						is_faction_leader = no
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							ROOT = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					remove_from_faction = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
}

	}

		name = kmt.25.b
		remove_from_faction = MON
		MON = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = false_document_trusted
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.26 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = MON
				modifier = never_like_them_anyway
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = kmt.25.c
		remove_from_faction = MON

			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT

			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.26 }
		}
		ROOT = {

				target = MON
				modifier = never_like_them_anyway
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MON
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

#great leap furnace auto build
country_event = {
	id = kmt.40
	title = kmt.40.t
	desc = kmt.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_burma_road

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 50
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PRC
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = shitty_furnace_state
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = kmt.40.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:shitty_furnace_state = {
				set_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
			}
		}
	}
}



country_event = {
	id = kmt.41
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = KMT_great_leap_started
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = PRC
						is_owned_by = PRC
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_core_of = PRC
					is_owned_by = PRC
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = KMT_fully_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}

	option = {}
}






#famine
country_event = {
	id = kmt.43
	title = kmt.43.t
	desc = kmt.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 73
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
		}
		has_country_flag = commune_visited
		tag = PRC
		any_state = {
			has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = KMT_shitty_furnaced
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
				set_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
						has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
					}
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.43.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = KMT_great_leap_famine
				}
				add_manpower = -100000
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
					has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
				}
			}
			add_ideas = KMT_great_leap_famine_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.44 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

					is_in_faction_with = SOV

					is_puppet_of = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = TAN

					tag = SIK
				}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				all_owned_state = {
					all_neighbor_state = {
						NOT = {

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			}

			}

				has_war_with = FRA

				has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
			}
		}
		AND = {
			728 = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						owner = { tag = FRA }
						controller = { tag = FRA }
					}
					AND = {
						owner = { tag = FRA }
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag
						}
					}
				}
			}
			670 = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						owner = { tag = FRA }

					}
					AND = {
						owner = { tag = FRA }
						controller = {
							has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war
							has_country_flag = gzw_war_flag

			}

		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = kmt_demand_indochina_war

				white_peace = FRA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					728 = {
						owner = {
							tag = FRA
						}

						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 728
			}

							tag = FRA
						}

					}

				transfer_state = 670
			}

#lower warlord clique penalty 3 left
country_event = {
	id = kmt.79
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PRC
			tag = CHI
			tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		NOT = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			AND = {
				has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
			OR = {
				has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
			}
		}
		check_for_warlord_full = no
		check_for_warlord_7_left = no
		check_for_warlord_6_left = no
		check_for_warlord_5_left = no
		check_for_warlord_4_left = no
		check_for_warlord_3_left = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
							has_war = yes
						}
						has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
		}
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
		add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
	}

	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.82
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = PRC
			tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				check_for_warlord_full = no
				check_for_warlord_7_left = no
				check_for_warlord_6_left = no
				check_for_warlord_5_left = no
				check_for_warlord_4_left = no
				check_for_warlord_3_left = no
				check_for_warlord_2_left = no
				check_for_warlord_1_left = no
				check_for_warlord_none = yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
							has_war = yes
						}
						has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
		}
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
	}
	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.83
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
		}
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = PRC
			tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		has_war = yes
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
		}
		OR = {
			OR = {
				GXC = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				YUN = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				XSM = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				SHX = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			}
			OR = {
				GXC = { exists = no }
				YUN = { exists = no }
				XSM = { exists = no }
				SHX = { exists = no }
			}
			OR = {
				GXC = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
				YUN = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
				XSM = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
				SHX = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
		add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
	}
	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.179
	title = kmt.179.t
	desc = kmt.179.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_british_artillery

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = kmt179_triggered
		}
		has_country_flag = incom_indus_ready
		has_tech = basic_machine_tools
		OR = {
			has_tech = concentrated_industry
			has_tech = dispersed_industry
		}
		has_tech = construction1
		OR = {
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 50
				has_war = no
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 65
				has_defensive_war = yes
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_factories > 75
				has_offensive_war = yes
			}
		}
		has_idea = incompetent_industry_real
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.179.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = kmt_incompetent_indus_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = incompetent_industry_real
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = incompetent_industry_real
				add_idea = incompetent_industry_real_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = incompetent_industry_real_navy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = incompetent_industry_real_navy
				add_idea = incompetent_industry_real_2_navy
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = kmt179_triggered
	}
}

				has_defensive_war = yes

				has_offensive_war = yes
			}

		NOT = {
			has_idea = public_iliteracy

#enemy close
country_event = {
	id = kmt.203
	title = kmt.203.t
	desc = kmt.203.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = await_decision_tr
			has_country_flag = treasures_abroad
			has_country_flag = treasure_ransacked
			has_country_flag = no_transfer_tr
		}
		event_target:KMT_treasure_state = {
			OR = {
				any_neighbor_state = {
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.203.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_treasure_state = {
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = kmt_national_treasure_ransacked
				days = 900
			}
			set_country_flag = treasure_ransacked
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = kmt_defend_the_treasures
					days = 365
				}
				set_country_flag = no_transfer_tr
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.203.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 613 }
			}
			clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
			605 = {
				save_global_event_target_as = KMT_treasure_state
				custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_will_be_destination_tt
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 605 }
					}
					clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
					325 = {
						save_global_event_target_as = KMT_treasure_state
						custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_will_be_destination_tt
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:KMT_treasure_state = { state = 325 }
							}
							clear_global_event_target = KMT_treasure_state
							add_timed_idea = {
								idea = KMT_treasure_abroad_idea
								days = 365
							}
							set_country_flag = treasures_abroad
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = await_decision_tr
	}
}

		tag = CHI
		num_of_controlled_states < 2
		524 = {
			owner = { tag = CHI }
			controller = { tag = CHI }
		}
		has_war_with = PRC
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_controlled_states < 2
				524 = {
					owner = { tag = CHI }
					controller = { tag = CHI }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = kmt.217 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#status quo force peace
country_event = {
	id = kmt.217
	title = kmt.217.t
	desc = kmt.217.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		num_of_controlled_states < 2
		524 = {
			owner = { tag = CHI }
			controller = { tag = CHI }
		}
		has_war_with = PRC
	}

	immediate = {
		PRC = {
			white_peace = CHI
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner =  { tag = CHI }
					NOT = {
						state = 524
					}
				}
				PRC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = CHI
					is_core_of = PRC
				}
				CHI = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_harsh_takeover
			remove_ideas = KMT_jinyuanquan_inflation
			remove_ideas = PRC_land_reform_stimulated_our_farmers
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.217.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_harsh_takeover
			remove_ideas = KMT_jinyuanquan_inflation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		}
	}
}

#colonies break free
country_event = {
	id = kmt.248
	title = kmt.248.t
	desc = kmt.248.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = kmt.248.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ENG
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MAL
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = FRA
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = VIN
				type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CAM
				type = annex_everything
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = LAO
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HOL
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = INS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kmt.248.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

		}

		}

			}
		}

#liberate vin?
country_event = {
	id = kmt.254
	title = kmt.254.t
	desc = kmt.254.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running

	trigger = {
		CHI = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		}
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = VIN
			owner = {
				NOT = { tag = VIN }
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		VIN = {
			exists = no
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.254.a
		VIN = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							is_in_faction_with = CHI
						}
					}
					is_core_of = VIN
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = VIN
					}
				}
				VIN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_technology = {
					gw_artillery = 1
					motorised_infantry = 1
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.5
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						VIN = { owns_state = 671 }
					}
					load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_671"
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						VIN = { owns_state = 286 }
					}
					load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_286"
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_together_with = CHI
					}
					VIN = {
						give_military_access = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.254.b
		VIN = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							is_in_faction_with = CHI
						}
					}
					is_core_of = VIN
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = VIN
					}
				}
				VIN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_technology = {
					gw_artillery = 1
					motorised_infantry = 1
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.5
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						VIN = { owns_state = 671 }
					}
					load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_671"
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						VIN = { owns_state = 286 }
					}
					load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_286"
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_together_with = CHI
					}
					VIN = {
						give_military_access = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			puppet = VIN
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.254.c
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.258
	title = kmt.258.t
	desc = kmt.258.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running

	trigger = {
		CHI = {
			has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		}
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = INS
			owner = {
				NOT = { tag = INS }
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		INS = {
			exists = no
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {
		name = kmt.254.a
		INS = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							is_in_faction_with = CHI
						}
					}
					is_core_of = INS
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = INS
					}
				}
				INS = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_technology = {
					gw_artillery = 1
					motorised_infantry = 1
				}

				}

#free raj?
country_event = {
	id = kmt.259
	title = kmt.259.t
	desc = kmt.259.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		RAJ = {
			has_war_with = CHI
			has_capitulated = yes
			is_puppet = yes
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	option = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
					has_government = fascism
				}
				puppet = RAJ
				end_puppet = RAJ
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_country = {
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war = no
					}
					puppet = RAJ
					end_puppet = RAJ
				}
			}
		}
		name = kmt.259.a
		transfer_state = 434
		434 = {
			add_core_of = CHI
			remove_core_of = RAJ
		}
		transfer_state = 441
		441 = {
			add_core_of = CHI
			remove_core_of = RAJ
		}
		ENG = {
			end_puppet = RAJ
			remove_from_faction = RAJ
		}
		RAJ = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = RAJ
					}
					RAJ = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.5
				}
				set_technology = {
					tech_military_police = 1
					tech_mountaineers = 1
					motorised_infantry = 1
				}
				load_oob = "RAJ_nationalist_army_otc"
			}
			321 = {
				add_core_of = RAJ
			}
			320 = {
				add_core_of = RAJ
			}
			RAJ = {
				transfer_state = 321
				transfer_state = 320
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_together_with = CHI
			}
			RAJ = {
				give_military_access = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = kmt.254.b
		transfer_state = 434
		434 = {
			add_core_of = CHI
			remove_core_of = RAJ
		}
		transfer_state = 441
		441 = {
			add_core_of = CHI
			remove_core_of = RAJ
		}
		ENG = {
			end_puppet = RAJ
			remove_from_faction = RAJ
		}
		CHI = {
			puppet = RAJ
		}
		RAJ = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = RAJ
					}
					RAJ = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.5
				}
				set_technology = {
					tech_military_police = 1
					tech_mountaineers = 1
					motorised_infantry = 1
				}
				load_oob = "RAJ_nationalist_army_otc"
			}
			321 = {
				add_core_of = RAJ
			}
			320 = {
				add_core_of = RAJ
			}
			RAJ = {
				transfer_state = 321
				transfer_state = 320
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_together_with = CHI
			}
			RAJ = {
				give_military_access = PREV
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.263
	title = kmt.263.t
	desc = kmt.263.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		country_exists = VIN
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = VIN
			owner = {
				has_war_with = CHI
				NOT = { tag = VIN }
			}
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					is_puppet_of = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		tag = CHI
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			VIN = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						controller = {
							OR = {
								tag = CHI
								is_in_faction_with = CHI
								is_puppet_of = CHI
							}
						}
						is_core_of = VIN
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = VIN
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = liberated_vin_state
					VIN = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:liberated_vin_state = { state = 286 }
							}
							VIN = {
								load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_286"
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								event_target:liberated_vin_state = { state = 671 }
							}
							VIN = {
								load_oob = "VIN_nationalist_army_671"
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.263.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			VIN = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						controller = {
							OR = {
								tag = CHI
								is_in_faction_with = CHI
							}
						}
						is_core_of = VIN
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = VIN
						}
					}
					VIN = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#peace w/ colonisers
country_event = {
	id = kmt.266
	title = kmt.266.t
	desc = kmt.266.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_europe_pact

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = KMT_oust_the_colonizers
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = VIN
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = VIN
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = LAO
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = LAO
				}
			}

	desc = kmt.279.d

		}

					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = KMT_implement_parliamentary_system
					}
					any_state = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
						}
					}
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
						has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
						has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
						has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.75
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = KMT_implement_parliamentary_system
						}
						any_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							NOT = {
								is_owned_by = ROOT
							}
						}
						OR = {
							has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
							has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
							has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
							has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
						}
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = KMT_kmt_party_name name = KMT_kmt_party_name }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Chiang Kai-Shek"
			desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI-SHEK_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/r56_portrait_CHI_Chiang_Kai_Shek.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = {
				army_connections
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.279.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_lesser
				}
			}
			add_ideas = civilian_economy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime
					has_idea = KMT_corrupted_government_wartime_lesser
				}
			}

		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7

			}
		}
		check_for_warlord_full = no
		check_for_warlord_7_left = no
		check_for_warlord_6_left = no
		check_for_warlord_5_left = no
		check_for_warlord_4_left = yes
	}

							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war

					}
				}

		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5

	id = kmt.288
	title = kmt.288.t
	desc = kmt.288.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_ace_died

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.290 }
			}
			CHI = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.291 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					408 = {
						controller = {
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = USA
								tag = USA
								is_puppet_of = USA
							}
						}
					}
				}
				408 = {
					owner = {
						country_event = { id = kmt.292 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = kmt.288.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = KMT_doolittle_raid
			days = 600
		}
	}
}

	id = kmt.292

	desc = kmt.292.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_001

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				same_ideo_with_USA = no
				add = 25
			}
		}
		name = kmt.292.a
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.295 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						NOT = {
							tag = SOV
						}
					}
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_detained
				}
				else = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						target = ROOT
						modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_detained_SOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				same_ideo_with_USA = yes
				factor = 75
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = USA
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = kmt.292.b
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.294 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.296 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help_JAP_reaction
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				is_puppet_of = JAP
				factor = 100
			}
		}

			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}

			country_event = { id = kmt.297 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_given_to_JAP
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.298 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = KMT_doolittle_pilots_help_arrest
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = kmt.301
	title = kmt.301.t
	desc = {
		text = kmt.301.d_1
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.301.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = PRC_civil_war_started
		OR = {
			tag = SHX
			tag = YUN
			tag = GXC
			tag = XSM
		}
		CHI = {
			has_war_with = PRC
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = KMT_PRC_joined
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.301.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = CHI
				enemy = PRC
			}
			CHI = {
				country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
			}
			else = {
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.302 }
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.301.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#lower warlord clique penalty 7 left
country_event = {
	id = kmt.317
	hidden = yes


	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = PRC
			tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		NOT = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
			AND = {
				has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
			has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
			OR = {
				has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
			}
		}
		check_for_warlord_full = no
		check_for_warlord_7_left = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
							has_war = yes
						}
						has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
		}
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
		remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5

				}

		is_puppet = no

			has_country_flag = event325_fired
			has_global_flag = KMT_united_front_enabled

#scorch earth
country_event = {
	id = kmt.328
	title = kmt.328.t
	desc = kmt.328.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_1
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_2
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_3
			has_idea = KMT_lure_them_in_4
		}
		any_state = {
			is_owned_by = ROOT
			controller = {
				has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = scorched
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					controller = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				set_state_flag = scorched
				set_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.328.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = scorched_tt
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 4
				}
				clr_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = scorched_tt
			}
			clr_state_flag = scorched_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.330
	title = kmt.330.t
	desc = kmt.330.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_german_advisors_remain

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		OR = {
			has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
			has_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GER
			GER = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = CHI
					value < -5
				}
			}
			has_opinion = {
				target = GER
				value < -5
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = { id = kmt.331 }}
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.330.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			remove_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
		}
	}
}

#china request sino-german joint
country_event = {
	id = kmt.332
	title = kmt.332.t
	desc = kmt.332.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.332.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CHI
			modifier = more_sino_german_coop
		}
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = more_sino_german_coop
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = german_advisors
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = german_advisors
					add_idea = KMT_sino_german_joint_research_ger_adv
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = KMT_sino_german_joint_research
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = KMT_german_approved
			country_event = {
				id = kmt.333
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.332.b
		CHI = {
			country_event = {
				id = kmt.334
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = {
		text = kmt.339.d_rep_killed
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CQ_send_rep
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.339.d_fight
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CQ_send_troops
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.339.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CQ_send_troops
			}
			add_manpower = -100
			army_experience = 1
			else = {
				FROM = {
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
							country_event = { id = wd.1 }
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ROOT
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				remove_from_faction = FROM
				FROM = {
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_war_together_with = ROOT
							}
							country_event = { id = wd.1 }
						}
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = FROM
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = KMT_stall_time
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = kmt.344.d_c
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_seek_cob
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		name = kmt.343.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_CQ_stall_time_tt
		set_country_flag = PRC_stall_time
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
		}
		name = kmt.344.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_together_with = FROM
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = wd.1 }
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.345 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = kmt.344.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = KMT_seek_cob
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PRC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				create_faction = KMT_united_chinese_gov
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				add_ai_strategy = {
					id = "PRC"
					type = alliance
					value = 200
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						PRC = {
							every_unit_leader = {
								set_nationality = CHI
							}						
						}

					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.346 hours = 2 }
		}
	}
}

#retreat to taiwan
country_event = {
	id = kmt.347
	title = kmt.347.t
	desc = kmt.347.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		524 = {
			owner = { tag = ROOT }
			controller = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			any_country = {
				NOT = { tag = PRC }
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		PRC = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			is_puppet = no
		}
		OR = {
			num_of_controlled_states < 4
			surrender_progress > 0.89
		}
		has_global_flag = PRC_restart_chinese_civil_war
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				NOT = {
					state = 524
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		add_ideas = KMT_retreat_to_taiwan_idea
		set_capital = 524
		add_political_power = -50
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
		name = kmt.347.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kmt.348
	title = kmt.348.t
	desc =  kmt.348.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			any_country = {
				NOT = {
					tag = PRC
				}
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		has_war_with = PRC
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				any_state = {
					region = 165
					controller = { tag = PRC }
				}
				OR = {
					613 = { controller = { tag = PRC }}
					596 = { controller = { tag = PRC }}
					595 = { controller = { tag = PRC }}
					600 = { controller = { tag = PRC }}
				}
			}
		}
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 3
			AND = {
				owns_state = 598
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 598
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 606
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 606
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 620
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 620
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 605
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 605
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owns_state = 601
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 601
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.348.a
		PRC = {
			country_event = { id = kmt.212 hours = 5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 145
							region = 144
							region = 143
							region = 155
							AND = {
								region = 164
								OR = {
									state = 620
									state = 607
									state = 606
									state = 598
								}
							}
						}
						owner = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_puppet_of = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					PRC = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kmt.347.b
	}
}

		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kmt.358.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = CHI_KR_fd
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
				}
				puppet = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = CHI_KR_fd
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
